And what does it really imply?\nLet's try and find some answers by participating in The Agri'Food Collage workshop. Directly inspired by The Climate Fresk, The Agri'Food Collage is a scientific and creative workshop designed to acquire as a team an overview of the issues weighing on our food supply, and discuss the actions to be taken to turn it into a solutions platform.\nDeveloped in partnership with ADEME \u2013 the French agency for the ecological transition, The Agri'Food Collage is based on over 150 reference documents and the contribution of experts from the many fields related to our food: environment, economy, society, ... and a bit of history too! See it as the agri-food system \"serious game\", based on collective intelligence and extremely educational because it allows you to learn a lot in a very short time, whether you're just curious or already knowledgeable.\nIt is also an opportunity to meet other people interested in the subject of the sustainability of our food, and to discover an effective tool to raise awareness and catalyze transformative action around you.\nAgenda & Practical Info\n  Workshop language : English.\n  Group introduction\nReconstruction of the Agri'Food Collage\nDebrief\nShare actions ideas\n  Recommended age: 16 and above.\nThis workshop will be held online via videoconference, and we'll be using a web-based visual collaboration tool. Aucun pr\u00e9requis n'est demand\u00e9 pour faire l'atelier !\nD\u00e9roul\u00e9\nL\u2019atelier dure environ 3h et se d\u00e9coupe en plusieurs \u00e9tapes :\nD\u00e9marrage (30 min) : icebreaker, pr\u00e9sentation des participant.e.s, de l\u2019animateur.rice, de l\u2019atelier, \u2026\nR\u00e9flexion (1h15) : \u00e9tude des causes et cons\u00e9quences de nos consommations sur le climat, la biodiversit\u00e9, la sant\u00e9 et la r\u00e9silience alimentaire\nSolutions (30 min) : quelles solutions pouvons-nous mettre en place d\u00e8s maintenant \u00e0 notre \u00e9chelle pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable ? Quelles sont leurs cons\u00e9quences ?\nActions (30 min) : choix d\u2019une action individuelle et une action collective pour tendre vers une alimentation plus durable et anticipation des difficult\u00e9s/freins qui pourraient \u00eatre rencontr\u00e9s\nD\u00e9brief (15 min) : retours sur l\u2019atelier, derniers conseils, quelle suite donner \u00e0 l\u2019atelier, ...\nCroyez-nous, \u00e7a passe (tr\u00e8s) vite !\nInfos pratiques\nMat\u00e9riel\nVous aurez simplement besoin d\u2019un ordinateur, d\u2019un micro et d\u2019une connexion internet suffisante pour pouvoir \u00e9changer avec les autres participant.e.s. In our clothing, furniture, toys and even computers! But how much do you really know about them? What exactly are our textiles made from? How sustainable are they, really? How far do our clothes travel before we buy them? Where do they go once they are donated?\n  This collaborative workshop illustrates the complexities and impacts (social and ecological) of the textile industry by using clothing as a case study. You will create the production chain of textiles, learn about the industry\u2019s impact, and then work together to find solutions and actions you can take.\n  This workshop is inspired by the pedagogy of the Climate Fresk (an interactive workshop that teaches the IPCC Climate report). Experience this unique way of learning, if you are new to the Fresk universe of workshops. Launched in 2021, Textiles UnTangled has been enjoyed by over 600 participants.\n  You will learn:\n  1. Materials 101 - What fabrics should I choose!?!\n2. The life cycle of textiles, from raw materials to end of life\n3. Textile industry impacts on the planet and on humans.\n4. How to think critically of claims made by companies & organizations about their sustainability\n5. Notions of circular economy, systems view thinking, and human centered solutions\n6. Actions that can be taken on a collective, business, and individual level\nAll while working together and having fun!\n  Our main sources: Ellen MacArthur Foundation, Preferred Textiles Report, OXFAM, Fashion Revolution and ADEME.\n  What participants have said:\n  \"This game is a fun, civic-minded and inclusive way to think about our relationship to clothing. They are professionals, experts and concerned citizens of many backgrounds. Inspired by the Climate Fresk, the workshop will allow you to understand the issues surrounding our use of natural resources and our generation and treatment of waste as well as other impacts caused by human activities. The workshop lasts 3 hours and takes place in groups of 6/7 people with 1 facilitator.\nThe Circular Economy Collage workshops are aimed at the general public, and are open to all, whatever your level of knowledge on these subjects. The Collage is also relevant for other audiences such as companies, communities and schools.  For our public workshops, participation is limited to 1 participant per organisation. If several members of your organisation wish to take part, please contact us to organise a dedicated session.\nBenefits of the workshop\nHaving deepened your understanding of the limits of the linear production-consumption-waste system, you will discover a more virtuous model for our economy and lots of ways that each of us can save natural resources and produce less waste. You will leave the workshop more aware, better-informed and motivated to take action to \"circularise\" our system!",
